cybrom
​Cybrom Technology Pvt. Ltd., established in 2007 and headquartered in Bhopal, Madhya Pradesh, is a premier institute specializing in skill-based training and job-oriented upskilling. The institute offers a diverse range of courses, including Full Stack Development (Java, Python, PHP, MERN), Cyber Security, Machine Learning, Data Science, Red Hat, Cloud Computing, and CCNA. These programs are designed to equip students with the latest industry-relevant skills, ensuring they stay ahead in the rapidly evolving tech landscape. 

cybrom E&ICT
The institute's dedication to excellence is further exemplified by its collaborations with esteemed organizations, such as the E&ICT Academy at IIT Guwahati, enhancing the credibility and recognition of its courses. With a proven track record of placing over 1,500 trained candidates in reputable companies, Cybrom continues to be a trusted partner for individuals aspiring to build successful careers in the IT industry.

​Cybrom Technology

Machine Learning
Machine Learning is a subset of Artificial Intelligence that enables systems to learn from data, identify patterns, and make decisions with minimal human intervention

Machine Learning types
Supervised Learning: Models are trained on labeled data.​

Unsupervised Learning: Models work with unlabeled data to find hidden patterns.​

Reinforcement Learning: Models learn by receiving rewards or penalties for actions.
